class="top-container"> <div class="top-g"> <div class="webtop-g"> <span class="z">&nbsp;</span> <h2 class="h">bullying</h2> <span class="z">&nbsp;</span> <a id="3308d00765544510ad740fd8ee23fae3"></a><a href="entry://#18831010d63841aa99e3a4d6149b5efd" class="to-top"><span class="pos">noun</span></a> </div> <span class="pos-g"><span class="pos">noun</span></span> <div class="pron-gs ei-g"> <span class="pron-g" geo="br"><span class="prefix">BrE</span> <a class="sound audio_play_button pron-uk icon-audio" otitle=" pronunciation English" href="sound://media/english/uk_pron/b/bul/bully/bullying__gb_2.mp3" type="sound"> &nbsp; </a></span> <span class="sep">;</span> <span class="pron-g" geo="n_am"><span class="prefix">NAmE</span> <a class="sound audio_play_button pron-us icon-audio" otitle=" pronunciation American" href="sound://media/english/us_pron/b/bul/bully/bullying__us_2.mp3" type="sound"> &nbsp; </a></span> </div> <span class="gram-g"><span class="wrap">[</span><span class="gram">uncountable</span><span class="wrap">]</span></span> <div class="clear"> &nbsp; </div> <br> </div> </div> <span class="sn-gs"><span class="sn-g"><span class="def">a problem that is common in schools where some children use their strength or important positions to hurt or frighten smaller or weaker children. The people who do this are called <span class="ndv">bullies</span>. There are many books about British schools that describe how <span class="ndv">bullies</span> make other children unhappy in this way. The most famous <span class="ndv">bully</span> in English literature is <span class="ndv" type="deadxref">Flashman</span> in <span class="xr-g"><span class="ndv">Tom Brown's Schooldays</span></span>.</span></span></span> </div> </div></div></html>
